msg:The hotel environment is comfortable, the family room is cute and clean. The room has a cinema screen and includes iQiyi membership. My dad watched the Premier League live broadcast on the night we checked in.
The hotel service is good and check-in is quick. Since there were three of us adults, we called customer service to ask for an extra bath towel, which was delivered quickly. The Internet suddenly went offline while watching football in the evening. The hotel staff immediately helped us change rooms and even gave us snacks to apologize.
There is a coffee shop and a Chaoshan beef hot pot restaurant downstairs, so you don‚Äôt have to go far for dinner. It's easy to take a taxi and go to the high-speed rail station or Yuhou Street.
However, the breakfast arrangement needs to be improved. The restaurant is relatively small. There was a tour group on the first morning. I guess they left at 8 o'clock, so they occupied the entire restaurant at 7 o'clock. We had a hard time finding a seat (the table in the lobby was not open), and Food and drinks were not added in time, making it difficult to eat. When my mother was waiting for noodles, she was stood in line by someone. The person even yelled at her, saying she didn't stand in line because she was getting eggs. The quality of these elderly tour groups is very poor. The next day we went downstairs for breakfast after 8 o'clock to avoid this group of people and enjoy breakfast slowly. It is recommended that if the hotel receives a tour group, it first reminds the guests to have breakfast at a staggered time with the tour group or to provide additional seats.
